# Task List Snapshot - Coordinator Live Linear Snapshot-Only Retry Assignee-Identity Fallback (1322-coordinator-live-linear-snapshot-only-retry-assignee-identity-fallback) - Update 2026-03-24: opened as the narrow CO-9 remediation lane after auditing the current queued-retry ownership paths against the local Symphony baseline. The live-resolver path already behaves correctly because it evaluates both `viewer_id` and `assignee_id`, but the snapshot-only queued-retry fallback in `providerIssueHandoff.ts` reconstructs a tracked issue from persisted claim state with `viewer_id: null`.
